create or replace PROCEDURE BRF56_MAPPING_PROCEDURE (REPORT_DATE DATE)
IS
   V_REPORT_DATE DATE := To_date (REPORT_DATE, 'DD-MM-YYYY'); 

BEGIN
delete from BRF56_MAPPING_TABLE where report_date = v_report_date;
Commit;

--INSERT VALUES

INSERT INTO BRF56_MAPPING_TABLE
(CUST_ID,
FORACID,
ACCT_NAME,
ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,
GL_CODE,
GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE,
SCHM_CODE,
SCHM_TYPE,
SOL_ID,
ACID,
LEGAL_ENTITY_TYPE,
CONSTITUTION_CODE,
PURPOSE_OF_ADVN,
HNI_NETWORTH,
TURNOVER,
COUNTRY_OF_INCORP,
REPORT_DATE)
SELECT CUST_ID,ACCT_NUMBER,ACCT_NAME,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,GL_CODE,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE,
SCHM_CODE,SCHM_TYPE,SOL_ID,ACID,LEGAL_ENTITY_TYPE,CONSTITUTION_CODE,
PURPOSE_OF_ADVN,HNI_NETWORTH,TURNOVER,COUNTRY_OF_INCORP,REPORT_DATE FROM GENERAL_MASTER_TABLE
WHERE report_date = v_report_date and sol_id in ('9005','9004',  '9002', '9003', '9008',  '9001',
'9010') and  schm_type in ('SBA','CAA','ODA','CLA','LAA','PCA','FBA');

--IN UAE AND NON-UAE
INSERT INTO BRF56_MAPPING_TABLE
(CUST_ID,
FORACID,
ACCT_NAME,
ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,
GL_CODE,
GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE,
SCHM_CODE,
SCHM_TYPE,
SOL_ID,
ACID,
LEGAL_ENTITY_TYPE,
CONSTITUTION_CODE,
PURPOSE_OF_ADVN,
HNI_NETWORTH,
TURNOVER,
COUNTRY_OF_INCORP,
REPORT_DATE,BACID)
SELECT CUST_ID,ACCT_NUMBER,ACCT_NAME,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,GL_CODE,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE,
SCHM_CODE,SCHM_TYPE,SOL_ID,ACID,LEGAL_ENTITY_TYPE,CONSTITUTION_CODE,
PURPOSE_OF_ADVN,HNI_NETWORTH,TURNOVER,COUNTRY_OF_INCORP,REPORT_DATE,BACID FROM GENERAL_MASTER_TABLE
WHERE report_date = v_report_date and sol_id in ('9005','9004',  '9002', '9003', '9008',  '9001',
'9010') and gl_sub_head_code in ('41101','41071','41131','41141','41101','41131') and gl_code in ('41100') and 
BACID IN ('41071001', '41101002','41131004', '41071018', '41071035','41071017','41141055','41131004','41141029','41071036','41131001',
'41101001') ;



--IN UAE AND NON-UAE ACCOUNTS
INSERT INTO BRF56_MAPPING_TABLE
(CUST_ID,FORACID,ACCT_NAME,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,GL_CODE,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE,SCHM_CODE,SCHM_TYPE,SOL_ID,ACID,
LEGAL_ENTITY_TYPE,CONSTITUTION_CODE,PURPOSE_OF_ADVN,HNI_NETWORTH,TURNOVER,COUNTRY_OF_INCORP,REPORT_DATE,BACID)
SELECT CUST_ID,ACCT_NUMBER,ACCT_NAME,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,GL_CODE,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE,
SCHM_CODE,SCHM_TYPE,SOL_ID,ACID,LEGAL_ENTITY_TYPE,CONSTITUTION_CODE,
PURPOSE_OF_ADVN,HNI_NETWORTH,TURNOVER,COUNTRY_OF_INCORP,REPORT_DATE,BACID FROM GENERAL_MASTER_TABLE
WHERE report_date = v_report_date and sol_id in ('9005','9004',  '9002', '9003', '9008',  '9001',
'9010') AND ACCT_NUMBER  LIKE '%141101003%' OR
ACCT_NUMBER LIKE '%1641051001%' OR
ACCT_NUMBER LIKE '%141051001%'OR
ACCT_NUMBER LIKE '%141071001%'OR
ACCT_NUMBER  LIKE '%1641101003%'OR
ACCT_NUMBER  LIKE '%1641101004%'OR
ACCT_NUMBER  LIKE '%141101003%'OR
ACCT_NUMBER LIKE '%141101004%'OR
ACCT_NUMBER  LIKE '%341051001%';


--ROW102 ABU DHABI
UPDATE BRF56_MAPPING_TABLE SET REPORT_NAME_1 ='BRF56' ,  REPORT_LABEL_1='ROW102' ,REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1= 'ROW102D'   
WHERE CONSTITUTION_CODE NOT IN ( '44101', '44102', '44103', '44104', '44105', '44106', '44107', '44108', '44109', 
'44110', '44111', '44112', '44113', '44114', '44115', '44116', '44199', '44201', 
'44202', '44203', '44204', '44205', '44206', '44207', '44208', '44209', '44210', 
'44211', '44212', '44213', '44214', '44215', '44216', '44217', '44299', '71005', 'HUFJT', 'INDL', 'INDL', 'INDVF', 
'INDVM', 'NREIN', 'RESIN', 'WPS') AND legal_entity_type NOT IN ('GOVTF', 'CGOVB', 'CB', 'GOVT', 'GOVTL', 'GOVTE', 'PSENO', 'PSEN', 'PSEC',
'PSECO') AND legal_entity_type IN ('NBFC', 'MXC') and sol_id in ('9001') AND COUNTRY_OF_INCORP  IN 'AE'; COMMIT;
UPDATE BRF56_MAPPING_TABLE SET REPORT_NAME_1 ='BRF56' ,  REPORT_LABEL_1='ROW102' ,REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1='ROW102E'  
WHERE CONSTITUTION_CODE NOT IN ( '44101', '44102', '44103', '44104', '44105', '44106', '44107', '44108', '44109', 
'44110', '44111', '44112', '44113', '44114', '44115', '44116', '44199', '44201', 
'44202', '44203', '44204', '44205', '44206', '44207', '44208', '44209', '44210', 
'44211', '44212', '44213', '44214', '44215', '44216', '44217', '44299', '71005', 'HUFJT', 'INDL', 'INDL', 'INDVF', 
'INDVM', 'NREIN', 'RESIN', 'WPS') AND legal_entity_type NOT IN ('GOVTF', 'CGOVB', 'CB', 'GOVT', 'GOVTL', 'GOVTE', 'PSENO', 'PSEN', 'PSEC',
'PSECO') AND legal_entity_type IN ('NBFC', 'MXC') and sol_id in ('9001') AND COUNTRY_OF_INCORP NOT IN 'AE'; COMMIT;
--ROW102 DUBAI
UPDATE BRF56_MAPPING_TABLE SET REPORT_NAME_1 ='BRF56' ,  REPORT_LABEL_1='ROW102' ,REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1='ROW102F'  
WHERE CONSTITUTION_CODE NOT IN ( '44101', '44102', '44103', '44104', '44105', '44106', '44107', '44108', '44109', 
'44110', '44111', '44112', '44113', '44114', '44115', '44116', '44199', '44201', 
'44202', '44203', '44204', '44205', '44206', '44207', '44208', '44209', '44210', 
'44211', '44212', '44213', '44214', '44215', '44216', '44217', '44299', '71005', 'HUFJT', 'INDL', 'INDL', 'INDVF', 
'INDVM', 'NREIN', 'RESIN', 'WPS') AND legal_entity_type NOT IN ('GOVTF', 'CGOVB', 'CB', 'GOVT', 'GOVTL', 'GOVTE', 'PSENO', 'PSEN', 'PSEC',
'PSECO') AND legal_entity_type IN ('NBFC', 'MXC') and sol_id in ('9003') AND COUNTRY_OF_INCORP  IN 'AE'; COMMIT;
UPDATE BRF56_MAPPING_TABLE SET REPORT_NAME_1 ='BRF56' ,  REPORT_LABEL_1='ROW102' ,REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1='ROW102G'  
WHERE CONSTITUTION_CODE NOT IN ( '44101', '44102', '44103', '44104', '44105', '44106', '44107', '44108', '44109', 
'44110', '44111', '44112', '44113', '44114', '44115', '44116', '44199', '44201', 
'44202', '44203', '44204', '44205', '44206', '44207', '44208', '44209', '44210', 
'44211', '44212', '44213', '44214', '44215', '44216', '44217', '44299', '71005', 'HUFJT', 'INDL', 'INDL', 'INDVF', 
'INDVM', 'NREIN', 'RESIN', 'WPS') AND legal_entity_type NOT IN ('GOVTF', 'CGOVB', 'CB', 'GOVT', 'GOVTL', 'GOVTE', 'PSENO', 'PSEN', 'PSEC',
'PSECO') AND legal_entity_type IN ('NBFC', 'MXC') and sol_id in ('9003') AND COUNTRY_OF_INCORP NOT IN 'AE'; COMMIT;
--ROW102 SHARJAH

create or replace PROCEDURE BRF56_DETAIL_PROCEDURE (REPORT_DATE DATE)
IS
   v_report_date   date := to_date (report_date, 'DD-MM-YYYY');
BEGIN


--Delete from BRF56_DETAILTABLE where REPORT_DATE = V_REPORT_DATE;
--Commit;


insert into BRF56_DETAILTABLE
( foracid, cust_id, ACCT_NAME,REPORT_DATE, REPORT_LABEL_1,REPORT_NAME_1,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1)
SELECT  foracid, CUST_ID, ACCT_NAME,REPORT_DATE,REPORT_LABEL_1,REPORT_NAME_1,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE, REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1 FROM 
brf56_mapping_table where REPORT_DATE = V_REPORT_DATE AND REPORT_LABEL_1 IS NOT NULL ;


MERGE INTO BRF56_DETAILTABLE A
USING ( SELECT ACCT_NUMBER, ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC FROM GENERAL_MASTER_TABLE) B
ON (A.foracid = B.ACCT_NUMBER)
WHEN MATCHED THEN
  UPDATE SET A.ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC = B.ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC;
  COMMIT;

COMMIT;
END;
